\DoxyCodeLine{00200\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00201\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ To\ support\ platform\ where\ unsigned\ long\ cannot\ be\ used\ interchangeably\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00202\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ inptr\_t\ (e.g.\ CHERI-\/extended\ ISAs),\ we\ can\ use\ the\ stdint.h\ intptr\_t.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00203\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Ideally,\ we\ could\ just\ use\ (u)intptr\_t\ everywhere,\ but\ this\ could\ result\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00204\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ ABI\ breakage\ if\ khronos\_uintptr\_t\ is\ changed\ from\ unsigned\ long\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00205\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ unsigned\ long\ long\ or\ similar\ (this\ results\ in\ different\ C++\ name\ mangling).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00206\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ To\ avoid\ changes\ for\ existing\ platforms,\ we\ restrict\ usage\ of\ intptr\_t\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00207\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ platforms\ where\ the\ size\ of\ a\ pointer\ is\ larger\ than\ the\ size\ of\ long.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00208\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00209\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ defined(\_\_SIZEOF\_LONG\_\_)\ \&\&\ defined(\_\_SIZEOF\_POINTER\_\_)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00210\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ \_\_SIZEOF\_POINTER\_\_\ >\ \_\_SIZEOF\_LONG\_\_}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00211\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define\ KHRONOS\_USE\_INTPTR\_T}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00212\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00213\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00214\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00215\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#elif\ defined(\_\_VMS\ )\ ||\ defined(\_\_sgi)}}
